 Uss kashtee kaa kya hoga jise maanjhee chhod gaya Patavare tod gaya  Desh ko aate hain pardesee log, bichhadate hain milate hain Aate jate hain yeh mausam, baag ujadate hain phir khilate hain Uss gulashan kaa kya hoga jise maalee chhod gaya Sab kaliya tod gaya, uss kashtee kaa kya hoga...
